### [329] [FEAST: Retrieval-Augmented Multi-Hierarchical Food Classification for the FoodEx2 System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03176)
*Lorenzo Molfetta,Alessio Cocchieri,Stefano Fantazzini,Giacomo Frisoni,Luca Ragazzi,Gianluca Moro*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: FEAST框架通过三阶段检索增强方法解决FoodEx2食品分类系统的复杂标签依赖、数据稀疏和极端输出维度问题，在稀有类别上显著超越基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FoodEx2食品分类系统在实际应用中面临复杂标签依赖、数据稀疏和极端输出维度的挑战，现有模型无法有效处理其实践约束，需要专门解决方案。

Method: 提出FEAST框架，将FoodEx2分类分解为三阶段：1)基础术语识别，2)多标签方面预测，3)方面描述符分配。利用层次结构指导训练，通过深度度量学习学习判别性嵌入。

Result: 在多语言FoodEx2基准测试中，FEAST在稀有类别上的F1分数比欧洲CNN基线提高了12-38%。

Conclusion: FEAST通过检索增强框架有效解决了FoodEx2系统的实践挑战，特别是缓解了数据稀疏问题并提升了稀有和细粒度标签的泛化能力。

Abstract: Hierarchical text classification (HTC) and extreme multi-label classification (XML) tasks face compounded challenges from complex label interdependencies, data sparsity, and extreme output dimensions. These challenges are exemplified in the European Food Safety Authority's FoodEx2 system-a standardized food classification framework essential for food consumption monitoring and contaminant exposure assessment across Europe. FoodEx2 coding transforms natural language food descriptions into a set of codes from multiple standardized hierarchies, but faces implementation barriers due to its complex structure. Given a food description (e.g., "organic yogurt''), the system identifies its base term ("yogurt''), all the applicable facet categories (e.g., "production method''), and then, every relevant facet descriptors to each category (e.g., "organic production''). While existing models perform adequately on well-balanced and semantically dense hierarchies, no work has been applied on the practical constraints imposed by the FoodEx2 system. The limited literature addressing such real-world scenarios further compounds these challenges. We propose FEAST (Food Embedding And Semantic Taxonomy), a novel retrieval-augmented framework that decomposes FoodEx2 classification into a three-stage approach: (1) base term identification, (2) multi-label facet prediction, and (3) facet descriptor assignment. By leveraging the system's hierarchical structure to guide training and performing deep metric learning, FEASTlearns discriminative embeddings that mitigate data sparsity and improve generalization on rare and fine-grained labels. Evaluated on the multilingual FoodEx2 benchmark, FEAST outperforms the prior European's CNN baseline F1 scores by 12-38 % on rare classes.

</details>

*Giovanni Pio Delvecchio,Lorenzo Molfetta,Gianluca Moro*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经符号AI作为实现人类水平智能的可能途径之一，虽然具有推断或利用行为模式的能力，但在语义泛化性和处理复杂领域方面存在局限。随着2017年以来连接主义系统的突破性进展，神经符号方法的竞争力受到质疑，特别是在自然语言处理和计算机视觉领域。因此需要系统调查神经符号方法在特定任务中的进展。

Method: 这是一篇调查综述论文，通过系统性地收集和分析神经符号AI领域的研究工作，特别是关注任务导向的方法。作者提供了详细的复现信息和深入评论，所有资料都通过GitHub仓库公开。

Result: 调查发现神经符号方法在增强可解释性和推理能力方面具有潜力，特别是在真实世界任务中。论文为研究人员提供了探索可解释神经符号方法的资源，涵盖了任务特定的进展和应用。

Conclusion: 神经符号AI仍然是增强AI系统可解释性和推理能力的重要方向。这篇调查旨在为研究人员提供实用资源，推动神经符号方法在真实世界场景中的应用和发展。

Abstract: The integration of symbolic computing with neural networks has intrigued researchers since the first theorizations of Artificial intelligence (AI). The ability of Neuro-Symbolic (NeSy) methods to infer or exploit behavioral schema has been widely considered as one of the possible proxies for human-level intelligence. However, the limited semantic generalizability and the challenges in declining complex domains with pre-defined patterns and rules hinder their practical implementation in real-world scenarios. The unprecedented results achieved by connectionist systems since the last AI breakthrough in 2017 have raised questions about the competitiveness of NeSy solutions, with particular emphasis on the Natural Language Processing and Computer Vision fields. This survey examines task-specific advancements in the NeSy domain to explore how incorporating symbolic systems can enhance explainability and reasoning capabilities. Our findings are meant to serve as a resource for researchers exploring explainable NeSy methodologies for real-life tasks and applications. Reproducibility details and in-depth comments on each surveyed research work are made available at https://github.com/disi-unibo-nlp/task-oriented-neuro-symbolic.git.

### [331] [Expectation and Acoustic Neural Network Representations Enhance Music Identification from Brain Activity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03190)
*Shogo Noguchi,Taketo Akama,Tai Nakamura,Shun Minamikawa,Natalia Polouliakh*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 使用ANN表示作为教师目标，区分声学和期望相关表征，可提升EEG音乐识别性能


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 音乐聆听时皮层活动编码声学和期望相关信息，ANN表征与皮层表征相似，可作为EEG识别的监督信号

Method: 将ANN的声学和期望相关表征作为教师目标，训练EEG识别模型；使用预训练模型预测这些表征，并组合不同表征

Conclusion: 教师表征类型影响下游性能，表征学习可由神经编码指导；期望表征反映超越起始或音高的预测结构，可扩展至大型数据集，为基于皮层编码原理的通用EEG模型奠定基础

Abstract: During music listening, cortical activity encodes both acoustic and expectation-related information. Prior work has shown that ANN representations resemble cortical representations and can serve as supervisory signals for EEG recognition. Here we show that distinguishing acoustic and expectation-related ANN representations as teacher targets improves EEG-based music identification. Models pretrained to predict either representation outperform non-pretrained baselines, and combining them yields complementary gains that exceed strong seed ensembles formed by varying random initializations. These findings show that teacher representation type shapes downstream performance and that representation learning can be guided by neural encoding. This work points toward advances in predictive music cognition and neural decoding. Our expectation representation, computed directly from raw signals without manual labels, reflects predictive structure beyond onset or pitch, enabling investigation of multilayer predictive encoding across diverse stimuli. Its scalability to large, diverse datasets further suggests potential for developing general-purpose EEG models grounded in cortical encoding principles.

### [332] [No Memorization, No Detection: Output Distribution-Based Contamination Detection in Small Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03203)
*Omer Sela*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CDD方法通过检测模型输出分布的集中度来识别数据污染，但其有效性取决于微调是否导致逐字记忆。当使用低秩适配等参数高效微调时，即使数据确实被污染，CDD也无法检测，因为模型没有记忆数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究CDD（基于输出分布的数据污染检测方法）在何种条件下有效或失效，特别是在不同微调策略下，理解数据污染检测的局限性。

Method: 在70M到410M参数的小语言模型上进行控制性污染实验，使用GSM8K、HumanEval和MATH数据集，比较不同微调方法（特别是低秩适配与全参数微调）对CDD检测效果的影响。

Result: CDD的有效性关键取决于微调是否产生逐字记忆。使用低秩适配时，模型可以从污染数据中学习但不记忆，此时CDD检测效果接近随机猜测。只有当微调容量足够大导致记忆时，CDD才能恢复较强的检测准确性。

Conclusion: 存在一个记忆阈值决定污染的可检测性，参数高效微调可能产生输出分布方法无法检测的数据污染，这对实际应用具有重要意义。

Abstract: CDD, or Contamination Detection via output Distribution, identifies data contamination by measuring the peakedness of a model's sampled outputs. We study the conditions under which this approach succeeds and fails on small language models ranging from 70M to 410M parameters. Using controlled contamination experiments on GSM8K, HumanEval, and MATH, we find that CDD's effectiveness depends critically on whether fine-tuning produces verbatim memorization. With low-rank adaptation, models can learn from contaminated data without memorizing it, and CDD performs at chance level even when the data is verifiably contaminated. Only when fine-tuning capacity is sufficient to induce memorization does CDD recover strong detection accuracy. Our results characterize a memorization threshold that governs detectability and highlight a practical consideration: parameter-efficient fine-tuning can produce contamination that output-distribution methods do not detect. Our code is available at https://github.com/Sela-Omer/Contamination-Detection-Small-LM

</details>

Abstract: Real-time proactive agentic system, capable of modeling Human State of Mind, using foundation EXG model and text embeddings model, running fully offline on the edge. Unlike all previously known systems, the NeuroSkill(tm) system leverages SKILL.md description of Human's State of Mind via API and CLI provided by the system, directly from the Brain-Computer Interface (BCI) devices, which records Human biophysical and brain signals. Our custom harness - NeuroLoop(tm) - utilizes all of the above to run agentic flow that manages to engage with the Human on multiple cognitive and affective levels of their State of Mind (e.g., empathy), by providing actionable tool calls and protocol execution with explicit or implicit requests from the Human. GPLv3 open-source software with ethically aligned AI100 licensing for the skill markdown.

### [334] [AI-for-Science Low-code Platform with Bayesian Adversarial Multi-Agent Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03233)
*Zihang Zeng,Jiaquan Zhang,Pengze Li,Yuan Qi,Xi Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种用于科学AI任务的贝叶斯对抗多智能体框架，通过三个LLM智能体（任务管理器、代码生成器、评估器）在对抗循环中协同工作，优化测试用例和代码生成，减少对LLM可靠性的依赖，并简化非专家用户的科学代码生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型在自动化科学代码生成方面具有潜力，但面临可靠性问题、多智能体工作流中的错误传播，以及在成功指标不明确的领域中的评估挑战。需要一种能够减少对LLM可靠性依赖、处理科学任务评估不确定性，并支持非专家用户协作的框架。

Method: 提出贝叶斯对抗多智能体框架，包含三个LLM智能体：任务管理器（将用户输入转化为可执行计划和自适应测试用例）、代码生成器（生成候选解决方案）、评估器（提供全面反馈）。通过对抗循环，任务管理器迭代优化测试用例挑战代码生成器，同时使用贝叶斯原理动态更新提示分布，整合代码质量指标（功能正确性、结构对齐、静态分析）。

Result: 基准评估显示LCP在生成鲁棒代码同时最小化错误传播方面有效。在地球科学跨学科任务测试中表现出强大的可靠性，优于竞争模型。平台能够将非专家提示转化为领域特定需求，无需手动提示工程。

Conclusion: 该贝叶斯对抗多智能体框架通过协同优化测试和代码，减少了对LLM可靠性的依赖，解决了科学任务固有的评估不确定性，同时通过低代码平台简化了人机协作，为非专家用户提供了有效的科学代码生成解决方案。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) demonstrate potentials for automating scientific code generation but face challenges in reliability, error propagation in multi-agent workflows, and evaluation in domains with ill-defined success metrics. We present a Bayesian adversarial multi-agent framework specifically designed for AI for Science (AI4S) tasks in the form of a Low-code Platform (LCP). Three LLM-based agents are coordinated under the Bayesian framework: a Task Manager that structures user inputs into actionable plans and adaptive test cases, a Code Generator that produces candidate solutions, and an Evaluator providing comprehensive feedback. The framework employs an adversarial loop where the Task Manager iteratively refines test cases to challenge the Code Generator, while prompt distributions are dynamically updated using Bayesian principles by integrating code quality metrics: functional correctness, structural alignment, and static analysis. This co-optimization of tests and code reduces dependence on LLM reliability and addresses evaluation uncertainty inherent to scientific tasks. LCP also streamlines human-AI collaboration by translating non-expert prompts into domain-specific requirements, bypassing the need for manual prompt engineering by practitioners without coding backgrounds. Benchmark evaluations demonstrate LCP's effectiveness in generating robust code while minimizing error propagation. The proposed platform is also tested on an Earth Science cross-disciplinary task and demonstrates strong reliability, outperforming competing models.

### [335] [Density-Guided Response Optimization: Community-Grounded Alignment via Implicit Acceptance Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03242)
*Patrick Gerard,Svitlana Volkova*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 论文提出DGRO方法，利用社区接受行为在表示空间中的几何结构作为隐式偏好信号，无需显式偏好标注即可对齐语言模型到社区规范。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对齐方法依赖显式偏好监督或预定义原则，但这对大多数在线社区（特别是缺乏机构支持、标注基础设施或围绕敏感话题的社区）不适用，因为偏好获取成本高、伦理问题多或文化不匹配。

Method: 提出密度引导响应优化（DGRO），利用社区接受行为在表示空间中形成的几何结构：被接受响应占据连贯的高密度区域，反映社区特定规范；被拒绝内容位于稀疏或不对齐区域。将这种结构作为隐式偏好信号进行对齐。

Result: 实验表明局部密度能恢复成对的社区判断，证明几何结构编码有意义的偏好信号。在标注稀缺的多样化社区中，DGRO对齐模型在人类标注者、领域专家和模型评估中均优于监督和提示基线。

Conclusion: DGRO为显式偏好监督不可用或与实际情况不匹配的社区提供了实用的对齐替代方案，并讨论了从涌现接受行为学习的意义和风险。

Abstract: Language models deployed in online communities must adapt to norms that vary across social, cultural, and domain-specific contexts. Prior alignment approaches rely on explicit preference supervision or predefined principles, which are effective for well-resourced settings but exclude most online communities -- particularly those without institutional backing, annotation infrastructure, or organized around sensitive topics -- where preference elicitation is costly, ethically fraught, or culturally misaligned.
  We observe that communities already express preferences implicitly through what content they accept, engage with, and allow to persist. We show that this acceptance behavior induces measurable geometric structure in representation space: accepted responses occupy coherent, high-density regions that reflect community-specific norms, while rejected content falls in sparser or misaligned areas. We operationalize this structure as an implicit preference signal for alignment and introduce density-guided response optimization (DGRO), a method that aligns language models to community norms without requiring explicit preference labels.
  Using labeled preference data, we demonstrate that local density recovers pairwise community judgments, indicating that geometric structure encodes meaningful preference signal. We then apply DGRO in annotation-scarce settings across diverse communities spanning platform, topic, and language. DGRO-aligned models consistently produce responses preferred by human annotators, domain experts, and model-based judges over supervised and prompt-based baselines. We position DGRO as a practical alignment alternative for communities where explicit preference supervision is unavailable or misaligned with situated practices, and discuss the implications and risks of learning from emergent acceptance behavior.

</details>


### [336] [Valet: A Standardized Testbed of Traditional Imperfect-Information Card Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03252)
*Mark Goadrich,Achille Morenville,Éric Piette*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Valet是一个包含21种传统不完全信息纸牌游戏的测试平台，用于标准化评估游戏AI算法在不同游戏类型中的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前不完全信息游戏AI算法通常只在单个游戏上进行性能比较，难以评估算法在不同游戏选择中的鲁棒性。纸牌游戏因其隐藏手牌和随机抽牌特性，是研究不完全信息的自然领域。

Method: 创建Valet测试平台，包含21种传统不完全信息纸牌游戏，涵盖多种类型、文化、玩家数量、牌组结构、机制、获胜条件以及信息隐藏和揭示方式。使用RECYCLE卡牌游戏描述语言标准化实现，通过随机模拟分析每个游戏的分支因子和持续时间，并报告蒙特卡洛树搜索玩家对抗随机对手的基线得分分布。

Result: Valet提供了一个多样化和全面的测试平台，包含21个经过标准化的不完全信息纸牌游戏。通过随机模拟获得了每个游戏的分支因子和持续时间特征，并建立了蒙特卡洛树搜索对抗随机对手的基线性能指标，证明了Valet作为基准测试套件的适用性。

Conclusion: Valet测试平台为不完全信息游戏AI算法的比较研究提供了标准化的评估环境，有助于促进游戏系统和算法在不同类型游戏中的鲁棒性评估和比较研究。

Abstract: AI algorithms for imperfect-information games are typically compared using performance metrics on individual games, making it difficult to assess robustness across game choices. Card games are a natural domain for imperfect information due to hidden hands and stochastic draws. To facilitate comparative research on imperfect-information game-playing algorithms and game systems, we introduce Valet, a diverse and comprehensive testbed of 21 traditional imperfect-information card games. These games span multiple genres, cultures, player counts, deck structures, mechanics, winning conditions, and methods of hiding and revealing information. To standardize implementations across systems, we encode the rules of each game in RECYCLE, a card game description language. We empirically characterize each game's branching factor and duration using random simulations, reporting baseline score distributions for a Monte Carlo Tree Search player against random opponents to demonstrate the suitability of Valet as a benchmarking suite.

</details>


### [337] [Inherited Goal Drift: Contextual Pressure Can Undermine Agentic Goals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03258)
*Achyutha Menon,Magnus Saebo,Tyler Crosse,Spencer Gibson,Eyon Jang,Diogo Cruz*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 现代语言模型代理在长上下文任务中仍存在目标漂移问题，虽然最新模型在对抗压力下表现稳健，但这种稳健性很脆弱，当用较弱代理的预填充轨迹进行条件化时会出现漂移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着语言模型作为代理在长上下文任务中的加速部署，需要深入理解目标漂移现象。虽然早期模型已显示出漂移倾向，但最新模型受影响程度尚不清楚，需要更新对漂移程度和原因的认知。

Method: 在模拟股票交易环境中测试最先进模型，研究对抗压力下的漂移行为。特别关注当模型用较弱代理的预填充轨迹进行条件化时的漂移继承现象。同时在新急诊室分诊环境中进行类似实验验证结果可迁移性。

Result: 最新模型在对抗压力下表现稳健，但这种稳健性很脆弱：当用较弱代理的预填充轨迹进行条件化时，相同模型经常继承漂移。漂移程度因模型系列而异，只有GPT-5.1在所有测试模型中保持一致的抗漂移能力。漂移行为在提示变体间不一致，与指令层次遵循行为相关性差。

Conclusion: 现代语言模型代理仍然容易受到上下文压力的影响，需要改进的后训练技术来缓解目标漂移问题。研究结果强调了跨不同环境漂移行为的可迁移性，以及开发更稳健代理的必要性。

Abstract: The accelerating adoption of language models (LMs) as agents for deployment in long-context tasks motivates a thorough understanding of goal drift: agents' tendency to deviate from an original objective. While prior-generation language model agents have been shown to be susceptible to drift, the extent to which drift affects more recent models remains unclear. In this work, we provide an updated characterization of the extent and causes of goal drift. We investigate drift in state-of-the-art models within a simulated stock-trading environment (Arike et al., 2025). These models are largely shown to be robust even when subjected to adversarial pressure. We show, however, that this robustness is brittle: across multiple settings, the same models often inherit drift when conditioned on prefilled trajectories from weaker agents. The extent of conditioning-induced drift varies significantly by model family, with only GPT-5.1 maintaining consistent resilience among tested models. We find that drift behavior is inconsistent between prompt variations and correlates poorly with instruction hierarchy following behavior, with strong hierarchy following failing to reliably predict resistance to drift. Finally, we run analogous experiments in a new emergency room triage environment to show preliminary evidence for the transferability of our results across qualitatively different settings. Our findings underscore the continued vulnerability of modern LM agents to contextual pressures and the need for refined post-training techniques to mitigate this.

</details>

### [338] [A survey of sampling discretization of integral and uniform norms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02459)
*F. Dai,E. Kosov,V. Temlyakov*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文综述了有限维空间中函数积分范数和一致范数采样离散化的最新进展，推广了经典Marcinkiewicz-Zygmund不等式，重点关注一般概率测度定义的范数及其离散逼近。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 采样离散化在傅里叶分析、插值和逼近理论中至关重要。经典Marcinkiewicz-Zygmund不等式为三角和代数多项式提供了基础，但需要推广到更一般的有限维空间和概率测度框架中。

Method: 采用综述研究方法，系统梳理作者近期研究成果及相关领域进展。重点展示证明中的核心思想和关键技术，作为已有三篇采样离散化综述论文的补充。

Result: 建立了有限维空间中函数范数采样离散化的理论框架，推广了经典结果，为更广泛的函数空间和测度提供了离散化方法。

Conclusion: 本文系统总结了采样离散化领域的最新发展，特别是作者的研究贡献，为相关领域研究者提供了重要的理论参考和技术指导。

Abstract: This paper surveys recent developments in the sampling discretization of integral and uniform norms for functions in general finite-dimensional spaces. These results generalize the classical Marcinkiewicz-Zygmund inequalities for trigonometric and algebraic polynomials, which play a crucial role in Fourier analysis, interpolation, and approximation theory. We focus on the problem in the broad context of finite-dimensional subspaces, where norms defined by general probability measures are approximated by their discrete counterparts.
  The primary emphasis is on results closely related to the authors' recent research. A key objective is to highlight the main ideas and techniques that form the foundation of the proofs in this area. This survey serves as a complement to three recently published survey papers on sampling discretization \cite{DPTT, KKLT, LMT}.

</details>


### [339] [Error analysis of scalar auxiliary variable finite element methods for the Landau--Lifshitz--Bloch equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02463)
*Agus L. Soenjaya*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 提出两种基于标量辅助变量(SAV)的有限元格式求解高温区Landau-Lifshitz-Bloch方程，分别采用半隐式欧拉和线性外推BDF2时间离散，均为线性、无条件稳定且满足离散能量定律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLB方程是描述铁磁体高温磁化动力学的成熟模型，但现有方法缺乏对高温区LLB方程的线性、能量稳定且具有二阶时间精度的数值格式，特别是针对这类拟线性向量值问题的严格误差分析。

Method: 提出两种完全离散的保形有限元格式：1) 基于半隐式欧拉时间离散的SAV方法；2) 基于线性外推BDF2方法的SAV格式。两种格式均为线性、无条件稳定，满足基于SAV能量泛函的离散能量定律。

Result: 在适当正则性假设下，证明了两种格式的无条件能量稳定性，并推导了在𝕃²、ℍ¹和𝕃∞范数下的最优阶误差估计。这是首次对拟线性向量值问题的完全离散SAV方法进行严格误差分析。

Conclusion: 成功开发了高温区LLB方程的第一个线性、能量稳定且具有二阶时间精度的数值格式，填补了该领域数值方法的空白，为高温磁化动力学模拟提供了可靠的计算工具。

Abstract: The Landau--Lifshitz--Bloch (LLB) equation is a well-established micromagnetic model for describing magnetisation dynamics in ferromagnets at elevated temperatures. In this paper, we propose and analyse two fully discrete, conforming finite element schemes based on the scalar auxiliary variable (SAV) approach for solving the LLB equation in the high-temperature regime above the Curie point. The first scheme employs a semi-implicit Euler time discretisation, while the second is based on a linearly extrapolated BDF2 method. Both schemes are linear, unconditionally stable with respect to the energy norm, and satisfy a discrete energy law involving the SAV-based energy functional that approximates the true micromagnetic energy. Under suitable regularity assumptions, we establish unconditional energy stability and derive optimal-order error estimates in $\mathbb{L}^2, \mathbb{H}^1$, and $\mathbb{L}^\infty$ norms. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first rigorous error analysis of a fully discrete SAV-based method for a quasilinear vector-valued problem, as well as the first linear, energy-stable scheme for the LLB equation in the high-temperature regime that achieves second-order temporal accuracy.

</details>


### [340] [Local Relaxation Fast Poisson Methods on Hierarchical Meshes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02763)
*Zhenli Xu,Qian Yin,Hongyu Zhou*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 提出了一种分层局部松弛（HLR）方法，用于加速泊松方程的求解。该方法通过局部无旋更新计算电场分布，同时严格满足高斯定律，并使用分层网格加速低频残差分量的收敛，达到O(NlogN)计算复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 泊松方程在计算物理中广泛存在，传统局部松弛算法收敛慢，特别是低频分量收敛困难。需要一种高效方法加速收敛，同时保持局部更新的优势。

Method: 将泊松方程转化为电场形式，通过逐单元扫描最小化相关电能，避免求解线性系统。引入分层网格结构，在局部无旋更新过程中加速低频残差分量的收敛。

Result: HLR方法在精度和效率方面表现良好，分层结构使计算复杂度达到O(NlogN)。在求解Poisson-Boltzmann和Poisson-Nernst-Planck方程的应用中显示出优越性能。

Conclusion: 分层局部松弛方法能有效加速泊松方程的求解，特别适用于需要频繁求解泊松方程的问题，具有高效、精确的特点。

Abstract: The local relaxation algorithm is promising for fast solution of Poisson's equations, which computes the electric field distribution in a stepwise manner via local curl-free updates while strictly enforcing Gauss's law. We propose a novel hierarchical local relaxation (HLR) method for speeding up the convergence of curl-free iterations. The local algorithm reformulates the Poisson's equation into the electric-field form and sweeps each cell to minimize the associate electric energy, avoiding the solution of linear systems. The updates with hierarchical meshes significantly accelerate the slow convergence of low-frequency components of the residual in the local curl-free update process. Convergence analysis is performed to obtain the convergence of the hierarchical relaxation approaches. Numerical results show that the HLR methods have the nice properties in accuracy and efficiency and the hierarchical construction leads to an overall computational complexity of $\mathcal{O}(N\log N)$ with respect to the number of grid points. Particularly, the applications in solving the Poisson--Boltzmann and Poisson--Nernst--Planck equations demonstrate the attractive performance for problems which frequently solve the Poisson's equations.

</details>


### [341] [On The Convergence of the Discretized Linear Static State-Based Peridynamic Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02916)
*Lukas Pflug,Michael Stingl,Max Zetzmann*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文证明了离散化线性状态型近场动力学系统的解收敛到连续解，并分析了常用网格自由离散化方法的收敛性


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究离散化近场动力学系统的收敛性，为实际数值模拟提供理论保证，特别是针对常用的网格自由离散化方法

Method: 首先分析离散化线性状态型静态近场动力学系统的收敛性，然后应用单点积分得到可实现的模型，该模型与常用的规则网格网格自由离散化方法一致，包括使用部分面积算法改进数值行为

Result: 证明了离散系统解收敛到连续解，对于文献中常用的固定权重函数和更强的输入数据假设，再次证明了收敛性，这些假设对实际应用并不显著限制

Conclusion: 为近场动力学数值模拟提供了严格的收敛性理论支持，特别是验证了常用网格自由离散化方法的数学可靠性，即使材料参数和外部体力存在不连续性也能适用

Abstract: In this paper, the convergence of the solutions for a discretized linear state-based static peridynamic system to the corresponding continuous solution is analytically proven. To obtain an implementable model, we further apply one-point-quadrature to the terms in the discrete equations. The resulting system coincides with the commonly used meshfree discretization using a regular lattice, including the possibility of using partial area algorithms to improve the numerical behavior. We again prove convergence, this time for fixed choices of a weighting function commonly used in literature and stronger assumptions on the input data. We note however, that these assumptions are not significantly restrictive for practical purposes. In particular, they still allow discontinuities in the material parameters and external body forces.

</details>


### [342] [Infinite dimensional generative sensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03196)
*Paolo Angella,Vito Paolo Pastore,Matteo Santacesaria*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了希尔伯特空间中生成式压缩感知的严格理论框架，将局部相干性概念扩展到无限维，证明了测量数只需与先验内在维度成正比即可稳定恢复，并通过达西流方程实验验证了理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度生成模型在逆问题中的理论保证大多局限于有限维向量空间，而物理信号通常建模为希尔伯特空间中的函数，这造成了理论与实际应用之间的差距。

Method: 将局部相干性概念扩展到无限维希尔伯特空间，推导出最优的、分辨率独立的采样分布；通过推广受限等距性质，建立生成式压缩感知的理论框架。

Result: 证明了稳定恢复所需的测量数只需与先验的内在维度成正比（最多相差对数因子），而与环境维度无关；数值实验显示在严重欠采样情况下，使用低分辨率生成器可作为隐式正则化器，提高重建稳定性。

Conclusion: 本文为希尔伯特空间中的生成式压缩感知提供了严格的理论基础，填补了有限维理论与无限维实际应用之间的空白，为物理信号建模提供了更贴近实际的理论保证。

Abstract: Deep generative models have become a standard for modeling priors for inverse problems, going beyond classical sparsity-based methods. However, existing theoretical guarantees are mostly confined to finite-dimensional vector spaces, creating a gap when the physical signals are modeled as functions in Hilbert spaces. This work presents a rigorous framework for generative compressed sensing in Hilbert spaces. We extend the notion of local coherence in an infinite-dimensional setting, to derive optimal, resolution-independent sampling distributions. Thanks to a generalization of the Restricted Isometry Property, we show that stable recovery holds when the number of measurements is proportional to the prior's intrinsic dimension (up to logarithmic factors), independent of the ambient dimension. Finally, numerical experiments on the Darcy flow equation validate our theoretical findings and demonstrate that in severely undersampled regimes, employing lower-resolution generators acts as an implicit regularizer, improving reconstruction stability.

</details>


### [343] [Physics-informed post-processing of stabilized finite element solutions for transient convection-dominated problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.03259)
*Süleyman Cengizci,Ömür Uğur,Srinivasan Natesan*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 提出一种混合计算框架，将PINN增强的SUPG方法扩展到瞬态问题，结合稳定有限元法和PINN修正策略，在终端时间选择性应用神经网络提升精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统方法在模拟对流主导的瞬态输运现象时面临计算挑战：经典离散方法产生虚假振荡，稳定化有限元方法需要额外正则化，而纯PINN方法难以捕捉对流主导区域的尖锐解结构且训练成本高。

Method: 提出PASSC方法的瞬态扩展，结合半离散稳定有限元法和PINN修正策略。使用SUPG格式和YZbeta激波捕捉算子进行稳定化，神经网络仅在终端时间附近选择性应用，利用最后K_s个时间快照增强有限元解，并强制满足控制方程和边界条件的残差约束。网络采用带随机傅里叶特征的残差块和自适应损失加权的渐进训练。

Result: 在五个基准问题（包括边界层、内层、行波和非线性Burgers动力学）上的数值实验表明，相比纯稳定有限元解，该方法在终端时间显著提高了精度。

Conclusion: 该混合框架成功将PINN增强的SUPG方法扩展到瞬态问题，通过选择性应用神经网络修正，有效解决了对流主导瞬态输运现象的数值模拟挑战，在终端时间获得了更精确的解。

Abstract: The numerical simulation of convection-dominated transient transport phenomena poses significant computational challenges due to sharp gradients and propagating fronts across the spatiotemporal domain. Classical discretization methods often generate spurious oscillations, requiring advanced stabilization techniques. However, even stabilized finite element methods may require additional regularization to accurately resolve localized steep layers. On the other hand, standalone physics-informed neural networks (PINNs) struggle to capture sharp solution structures in convection-dominated regimes and typically require a large number of training epochs. This work presents a hybrid computational framework that extends the PINN-Augmented SUPG with Shock-Capturing (PASSC) methodology from steady to unsteady problems. The approach combines a semi-discrete stabilized finite element method with a PINN-based correction strategy for transient convection-diffusion-reaction equations. Stabilization is achieved using the Streamline-Upwind Petrov-Galerkin (SUPG) formulation augmented with a YZbeta shock-capturing operator. Rather than training over the entire space-time domain, the neural network is applied selectively near the terminal time, enhancing the finite element solution using the last K_s temporal snapshots while enforcing residual constraints from the governing equations and boundary conditions. The network incorporates residual blocks with random Fourier features and employs progressive training with adaptive loss weighting. Numerical experiments on five benchmark problems, including boundary and interior layers, traveling waves, and nonlinear Burgers dynamics, demonstrate significant accuracy improvements at the terminal time compared to standalone stabilized finite element solutions.

</details>
